<h1 class="header"> <span class="itemprop" itemprop="name">Madonna</span>
</h1>
<div class="infobar" id="name-job-categories">
<a href="#soundtrack" onclick="nameJobCategoriesClickHandler(this)"> <span class="itemprop" itemprop="jobTitle">
Soundtrack</span></a> <span class="ghost">|</span>

<hr/>
<div class="txt-block" id="name-bio-text">
<div class="name-trivia-bio-text">
<div class="inline" itemprop="description">
The remarkable, hyper-ambitious Material Girl who never stops reinventing herself, Madonna is a seven-time Grammy Award-winner who has sold over three hundred million records and CDs to adoring fans worldwide. Her film career, however, is another story. Her performances have consistently drawn scathing or laughable reviews from film critics, and ...            <span class="see-more inline nobr-only">
<a href="/name/nm0000187/bio?ref_=nm_ov_bio_sm">See full bio</a> »
            </span>
</div> </div>
</div>
<div class="txt-block" id="name-born-info">
<h4 class="inline">Born:</h4>
<a href="/name/nm0000187/bio?ref_=nm_ov_bth_nm"> Madonna Louise Ciccone
</a> <br/>
<time datetime="1958-8-16" itemprop="birthDate">
<a href="/search/name?birth_monthday=8-16&amp;refine=birth_monthday&amp;ref_=nm_ov_bth_monthday">August 16</a>, 
     
<a href="/search/name?birth_year=1958&amp;ref_=nm_ov_bth_year">1958</a>
</time>
            in
            <a href="/search/name?birth_place=Bay+City%2C+Michigan%2C+USA&amp;ref_=nm_ov_bth_place">Bay City, Michigan, USA</a>
</div>
</td>

<h2>Did You Know?</h2>
<div class="see-more inline canwrap" id="dyk-personal-quote">
<h4 class="inline">Personal Quote:</h4>
I remember having conversations with <a href="/name/nm1042818?ref_=nm_dyk_qt1">Keith Haring</a> and with <a href="/name/nm0060016?ref_=nm_dyk_qt2">Jean Michel Basquiat</a> about the importance of your art being accessible to people. That was their big thing - it should be available to everyone.                    <span class="see-more inline">
<a href="/name/nm0000187/bio?ref_=nm_dyk_qt_sm#quotes">See more</a>
</span>
                    »
        </div>
<hr/>
<div class="see-more inline canwrap" id="dyk-trivia">
<h4 class="inline">Trivia:</h4>

</span>
                    »
        </div>
